Deng Yingsheng Appointed Commander of the New 13th Division 63

The Commander's Office is Located in Ji'an, Jiangxi Province

Nanchang Dispatch: The 16th Independent Brigade led by Deng Ying was originally under the command of Liu. Previously, Deng was engaged in suppressing bandits in the Ganjing Xinyu Yichun Jishui area and successively recovered Fenyi Yichun Yifeng Wanzai Gaoan and other counties. Liu considered that Deng's brigade had repeatedly achieved remarkable results in suppressing bandits and specially requested Chairman Chiang to expand the brigade into a division, with Deng being promoted to division commander. Chiang replied by telegram in winter, approving the request. Yesterday, Brigade Commander Deng also received a telegram from Liu Zhisheng from Xuzhou, appointing him as the commander of the newly编13th Division. The telegram read: "Urgent secret telegram to Deng Yingsheng, Commander of the 16th Independent Brigade, Jianhao Brother: The telegram from the Commander-in-Chief's Office in winter has been received. Deng Ying, Commander of the 16th Independent Brigade, is approved to be appointed as the commander of the newly編13th Division. The letter of appointment and official seal will be issued separately. I hope you will inform him and report on the new編情況, etc. I hereby telegram to comply with the order and hope you will take office and report as soon as possible. Liu Zhisheng Jiangping Seal." It is heard that the original編制 of Deng's brigade is not much different from the division headquarters. This time, it only needs to be slightly expanded to become a division. According to military sources, the three brigade commanders of the division will mostly be promoted from regimental commanders, and the regimental and battalion commanders will be promoted in turn. Deng himself is scheduled to take a Gan River steamer from the province to Zhangshu tomorrow (the 7th) to start the expansion. Once everything is ready, he will report his taking office. The division headquarters will be moved from Zhangshu to Ji'an because the overall headquarters for bandit suppression in the province has been moved from Ji'an back to Zhangshu. (May 6th)

Fifteen Gang Members from Haizhou Executed 64

Attached is Zhang Zhaohua's Confession

Suzhou Express: Fifteen gang members from Haizhou were executed by firing squad yesterday (the 8th) by the Taihu Bandit Suppression Headquarters. Their crimes are listed as follows:

Public Announcement: It is hereby announced that the Headquarters has successively captured the bandit leader Zhang Zhaohua and fifteen bandits including Wang, who have been interrogated separately. Their crimes of kidnapping for ransom and armed robbery have been confessed, and the rescued kidnap victims have testified in court that the facts are true. Moreover, they gathered in the lakes and resisted government troops, which violated Article 5 and Article 13 of the Provisional Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits. They have been presented to the Commander-in-Chief and sentenced to death. In addition to verifying their identities and binding them to the execution ground for execution by firing squad, this announcement is hereby made for public knowledge.

This announcement is made on the eighth day of May in the nineteenth year of the Republic of China.

Commander-in-Chief Hu Zuyu

The names of the fifteen gang members are as follows:

Zhang Zhaohua, 26 years old, from Huaiyin

Wang Peng, 38 years old, from Huaiyin

Qian Wenyuan, 30 years old, from Baoying

Xu Zhenqing, 30 years old, from Huaiyin

Miao Zichuan, 24 years old, from Haizhou

Liu Jinbiao, 35 years old, from Suqian

Xu Magao, 27 years old, from Huai'an

Huang Shifu, 30 years old, from Qingjiangpu

Qi Wenming, 34 years old, from Shuyang

Xiong Wenkui, 25 years old, from Suqian

Chen Siguan, 42 years old, from Pinghu

Jiang Yinquan, 54 years old, from Jinshan

Lu Jisheng, 40 years old, from Baoshan

Shen Jinlan, 26 years old, from Luodian

Shen Jinshan, 20 years old, from Liuhe

The confession of bandit leader Zhang Zhaohua is as follows:

(Question) Are you Gao Zian?

(Answer) Yes.

(Question) Do you have any other names? Aren't you called Zhang Zhaohua?

(Answer) I don't have any other names. You are called Zhang Zhaohua, and I am called Gao Zian.

(Question) Is your injury better?

(Answer) It's better, but I can't sit up.

(Question) People say you are Zhang Zhaohua, and I am Gao Zian. Being here is enough to be shot.

(Question) What did you do before?

(Answer) I used to work in the army. In 1927, I worked under Qian Shusheng, the director of the Jiangsu Water Police Department. Later, Director Qian was transferred to be the Haizhou Salt Affairs Supervisor, and I left the Water Police Department. In 1928, I was a brother in the Suzhou Water Police. Later, I worked in the first district of Shanghai until I took leave last August and lived in Gaochang Temple in Shanghai. Later, I moved to No. 104 Peide Lane, Datong Road. Because I was robbed by bandits, I moved to the countryside. I still have a child, so I often come to the countryside to see him. I have returned to my hometown several times in February.

(Question) Why did you become a bandit?

(Answer) It's a long story. The people in Shanghai are complex, and the judge must know that. I didn't do anything. When I lived in Shanghai, I made bad friends who led me to this point. What else can I say today? As for this time, I arrived at Shen Dian Bridge from Shanghai on the 13th of this month.

(Question) What is the name of your secretary?

(Answer) It is said that there is a secretary named Shen Jinshan. He used to run an opium den in Shanghai. But may I ask the judge, who said he was my secretary? (The judge said it was Shen himself who said so) Since Shen himself said so, I can tell you about this person. He used to study at Baode District Elementary School. Later, he worked in a Shanghai coal company. When the coal company closed down, he opened an opium den in Zhaiyu Lane. I met him last December. As for saying that he is my secretary, that is not accurate. Because inside, he only keeps accounts. All the plans are still made by Mao Zilong.

(Question) How did you get to know Mao Zilong?

(Answer) I also met him in Shen Jinshan's opium den.

(Question) Was Mao Zilong also on the boat that day? Where is he now?

(Answer) He was still on the boat when the firing started that day. Later, I don't know where he escaped to.

(Question) If you can tell us and help us catch Mao Zilong, we can help you atone for your sins.

(Answer) It is very difficult to catch Mao Zilong. Now that he knows that the situation is not good, he has long since moved from his home. Where can I find him now? Even when I usually want to meet him, he still has three or four rooms set up in the hotel. His personnel are hard to meet, let alone today.

(Question) Where did your weapons come from?

(Answer) The weapons were shipped back from Shanghai separately. In total, the Haizhou gang has no more than ten ships and more than one hundred people. These one hundred people all have weapons. Outsiders say that the Haizhou gang has hundreds of people. This is not reliable. Mao Zilong and I are very good friends. Is there anything about him that I don't know?

(Question) Now there are many people who can prove that you are Zhang Zhaohua, and even Shen Jinshan can confront you. Why don't you say it?

(Answer) My real name is Zhang Peiyao.

(Question) Perhaps you have several aliases, and Zhaohua is another one of your aliases. You might as well say it. You are a very capable person. If you tell the truth, our commander-in-chief can employ you. In the future, you can atone for your sins and do something for the country. Wouldn't that be good?

(Answer) There are also people outside who acknowledge that I am called Zhang Peiyao. The reason why I took leave last year was because of my bad temper.

(Question) Perhaps it is because your ability is superb and you are unwilling to be under others for a long time, so you want to join the bandits and seek a way out. But why bury your heroism?

(Answer) But I am not exaggerating. Many brothers know my heart. I always advise them not to rape women or abuse the hostages they capture. People should have a conscience. Women are other people's wives. If we rape them, we will not only insult them but also cause discord between them and their husbands. As for kidnapping hostages, it is nothing more than wanting money. Why abuse them? When I tell these things to my brothers, they are very moved. It is true that bandits are bad people, but we cannot completely deny everything. Who says that bandits are all heartless bad guys?

(Question) Outsiders say that you are Zhang Zhaohua. Is there anyone else besides you who is called Zhang Zhaohua?

(Answer) No one else is called Zhang Zhaohua. If there is Zhang Zhaohua, it is me.

(Question) Then naturally you are Zhang Zhaohua without a doubt. How many gangs are there inside you?

(Answer) Only the Haizhou gang. The rest don't have much strength.

(Question) Aren't there also the Henan gang, the Pudong gang, and the Anhui gang?

(Answer) Although these names exist, the Henan gang doesn't interact with us. Their leader is Tian Kuaizi. But their strength is not as great as the Haizhou gang. The Anhui gang has been eliminated since Wu Dajin was taken away and executed. As for the Pudong gang, I have never heard of them. I don't know what they are like. However, although the Haizhou gang is stronger than the Henan gang, it doesn't have the advantage of the Henan gang's position. Because many of the Henan people farm in the Great Lake. They can be bandits or ordinary people.

(Question) What kind of person is Mao Zilong?

(Answer) He is the most useless good-for-nothing.

(Question) How is Tian Kuaizi compared to Mao Zilong? How many guns does he have?

(Answer) Tian Kuaizi is better than him, but he also smokes opium. He smokes three or four ounces a day and even chews opium dross. As for his guns, he only has a dozen or so. But because he has the Big Sword Society as a foundation, his strength is not weak. When his subordinates gather, you can say there are hundreds of them. When they are dispersed, you can say there is not a single one because they are all farming in Taihu.

(Question) Are the four gangs commanded together?

(Answer) No, only each gang comes to help the Haizhou gang.

(Question) Shen Jinshan himself said that he is your secretary. Why do you say that he is just an accountant? (At this point, Shen was brought to the court. When Shen saw Zhang Zhaohua, he said, "Brigade Commander, you are here too." He said to the judge, "He is our Brigade Commander Zhang Zhaohua." Zhang then said to Shen, "I am the Brigade Commander, who are you?" Shen replied, "I am the secretary. Brigade Commander, we are people who do things with our heads held high. Even if we are arrested today, why should we hide it?" Zhang asked, "I don't know that you are the secretary. What kind of secretary are you? But I don't know who appointed me as the Brigade Commander. Who appointed us? You say it first." Shen replied, "We were appointed by the Reorganization Faction. Our mission is to accept the command of the Reorganization Faction." Zhang confessed, "But I must declare that after Shen Jinshan and I arrived on the boat, we never robbed anything, nor did we rape women, kill anyone, or set fires. We are confident of this." (The official asked) "Who from the Reorganization Faction contacted you?" (Answer) "Commander-in-Chief Xu, Commander-in-Chief Bai, and Ju Zheng. They all sent representatives several times indirectly to contact us." (Question) "Who were the representatives they sent to talk to you?" (Answer) "A certain Gao, from Haizhou." (Question) "Do you know Chen Tian (also known as Chen Shiqing) and Yan Fuchen? They are the commanders of the Fourth Detachment of the National Salvation Army." (Answer) "I don't know them and I don't recognize them." (Question) "How were you arrested that day?" (Answer) "When the firing started that day, I came out with three people because the bullets were exhausted and we couldn't continue firing. So we each escaped. We hired a small boat to Tianjing. We all slept in the cabin. The person rowing went directly to Tianjing Street. He went ashore to report that bandits had come. We got up and rowed the boat ourselves. Then came thirty or forty public security officers and opened fire on us. We rowed to Weiting and went to the homes of ordinary people to look for rice and boiling water. They all said they didn't have any. We went to a cave. The next day, before dawn, the public security officers came again and called us out of the cave. So the public security officers escorted us to Weiting, and then from Weiting to Suzhou." (Question) "Where were you injured?" (Answer) "I was injured on the boat while rowing." (Question) "How did you become a gang in the beginning?" (Answer) "Because I made bad friends in Shanghai, the people from Haizhou all called me to the lake. They said that there were so many brothers that we could form an army. So I came with them. A gentleman regrets before, a small man regrets after. I am just a small man, so I regret it today. I shouldn't have been with those bad guys." (Question) "It is said that you were completely exploited by the Reorganization Faction and lured by bad people to this point." (Answer) "However, I can't completely wrong others. I did it myself, so I will take responsibility myself. Why should I resent others? However, I ask the judge, they all followed me. Let me take responsibility for everything alone. There is no need to harm them. Just shoot me. We are also people who do things. I also ask the judge, please don't see us as bandits. We die for our cause. Our death is worthwhile. If you insist that we are bandits, we will not rest in peace even in death." (Shen Jinshan also made the same request: "Judge us as political prisoners. Don't punish us as bandits," etc.)

Songjiang 65

Supplementary election of standing committee members of the Xinzhuang Chamber of Commerce: Lv Shouhe, the standing committee member of the Xinzhuang Town Chamber of Commerce, was formerly vacant due to illness. Later, due to the occurrence of doubts, a request was submitted to the provincial government for interpretation. Wang Zhaoyun, the chairman of the chamber of commerce, has now scheduled a supplementary election on May 15th in accordance with the regulations. He has sent a letter to the district party headquarters and requested the county government to send personnel to supervise the election at that time in order to show solemnity.

Continuation of the Wang kidnapping case: After the theft and assault on Wang Ziqin's family in the eleventh map of Tianmashan, the detective team arrested the two criminals Yang Abu and Liu Jinyun, and recovered the stolen goods. Yesterday, they were brought to the county government for questioning and fully confessed. The victim was also summoned to identify them clearly on file. However, yesterday the county government questioned Yang Abu, who confessed that Wang Xiaodi, who lives in the city's east gate, was also an accomplice in the robbery. The bailiff then arrested Wang Xiaodi, who was brought to the county government for questioning today. According to Wang Xiaodi's confession, he did know Liu and others, but he did not know that they were thieves. The interrogator judged that Wang was suspicious and ordered him to be detained pending investigation.

Use of medicated wine for seedling planting: On the afternoon of the 7th, a pilgrim with a Zhejiang Jiaxing accent came to Maqi Temple in the city and claimed to be asking the temple monks to chant scriptures to pray for the ancestors. He carried food such as wine cakes and sesame cakes in his hands. When it was getting dark, the pilgrim planned to fill his stomach with sesame cakes and asked the incense burner to boil tea. He immediately took out a wine bottle and invited the Chen family's wife, who was nearly eighty years old and had been practicing in the temple for a long time, and the incense burner to drink with him. Unexpectedly, the wine was mixed with marijuana. After drinking it, they all became drowsy and lost all consciousness. When they woke up, they suddenly did not see the pilgrim. Upon checking, they found that Mrs. Chen's two gold ornaments and more than eighty yuan in cash had been lost. It was also a new type of seedling planting technique.

Suzhou 66

Higher Court plans to build a new prison: Lin, the president of the Higher Court, stated that the originally approved number of prisoners in the province was 13,000, but it has now increased to more than 20,000. The original number of the third sub-prison and detention center on Siqian Street of the Higher Court was 500, but there are now about 1,300 people detained, exceeding the approved number by more than half. Although the old arsenal at Shizikou outside Panmen has been rebuilt into a temporary shelter, it can only accommodate 300 more people, which still cannot be effectively疏通. Therefore, the site of the old silk weaving factory inside Panmen (the original site of the Gangyuan Bureau) has been surveyed and deemed suitable for the construction of a prison. Therefore, a draft plan has been drawn up and sent to the provincial government today (the 8th) to be submitted for discussion at the 292nd meeting of the provincial government tomorrow in order to facilitate疏通 and benefit prison administration.

Judgment in the murder and dismemberment case: Jia Zhengyi, the owner of the Jia Hengxing hardware store in Yangyu Lane, suffered from mental illness last year and killed his younger brother Jia Songshan with a hammer. He was sentenced to twenty years of imprisonment by the District Court yesterday and sent to the third prison on Siqian Street for execution.

Jiading 67

Reasons for the delay in the construction of long-distance telephones: In addition to the urban area and Loutang, where companies have successively laid long-distance telephones, the construction bureau has drafted a plan to set up six lines: Ji'an, Waihuang, Jiaxu, Jiaji, Xucao, and Chengguang. It will allocate special construction donations to pay for the expenses, together with the budget, and submit them to the county government for transfer to the construction bureau for approval. Later, the Construction Bureau instructed that the construction cost was too high and should be reduced. The bureau director should remake the budget according to the previous format and separately allocate the items. As for the use of special donations, a special case should be submitted for approval. Before the bureau's order to handle the matter is received and the source of funds is approved, no preparations should be made rashly. Therefore, this project still needs to be postponed.

Anting Township establishes a sanatorium: Anting Township Lantang Rural Normal School, recently joined with Kunshan Hospital to establish a rural sanatorium in the remaining rooms of the Kunqingjia Public Zhenchuan School. It is scheduled to open next week. Only registration fees will be charged, and medical fees will not be charged. It has internal and external acupuncture, emergency relief, and obstetrics departments. Replacement of the审判员: Zhang Mian, the judge of this county, has been transferred to Rugao by order of the Higher Court to clear up backlog cases. His vacancy has been filled by Zhuang Yongfang from Changzhou, who arrived in Jiading on the 7th to take office.

Each戒 forbade their children to go out. As a result, the number of students in each school suddenly decreased. Ships, and seized more than two taels of opium hidden in a fishing boat. The boat renter Zhu Yunchao was arrested and taken to the county government. Examiner Yang sentenced him to one year in prison and a fine of five hundred yuan.

Qingpu 69

Zhu Jizhou was not frightened to death: Chonggu Town in this county was tragically robbed on the 23rd of last month. When Zhu Jizhou, a resident of the town, was kidnapped, he was old and frightened, and his condition was like he was dying. The next day, a nameless corpse was found nearby. The people who saw it mistakenly thought it was Zhu, and the news spread far and wide. When his family heard the news, they went to see it, but it was gone. Later, it was learned that what they saw was an injured bandit who was lying on the riverbank. His clothes and age were the same as Zhu's, which caused the false rumor. Soon after, he was carried back by the bandit gang. At the moment, the Zhu family has received a confirmed report that the Nanhuitaiping Township security regiment has captured a bandit den and there is a hostage named Zhu Jizhou. They will go to that place to find a way to claim him.

Wuxi 70

One after another robbery cases in the county. Hua Luqing, a respected elder from Xizhuang Village in the northern part of the county, was robbed at his home the night before last. Mr. and Mrs. Hua were also burned by the thieves. It is learned that Tang Muxiao, a man of modest means residing near the Hangkou Lane of Taibo City, Houzhai, was suddenly beset by six or seven bandits wielding weapons at around 3 PM yesterday. The bandits forced open the door, swarmed in, ransacked the house, and wantonly looted. Gold ornaments, silver dollars, and clothing worth over 100 yuan were stolen. After acquiring the loot, the bandits noisily fled. Furthermore, at around 1 AM last night, over ten bandits armed with knives, clubs, flashlights, and the like, arrived at Guwanli Village near Dashuwan in Kaiyuan Township. They consecutively robbed four families, including those of Gu Shipei, Gong Wangrong, and Gu Alun, resulting in a total loss exceeding 1,000 yuan.

Active Clearance of Beggars. Since the establishment of the Vocational Training Center for Commoners in this county, the number of beggars has decreased, but thorough eradication has not been achieved. Male and female beggars still persistently beg from door to door in the market, disrupting public order. County Magistrate Sun Zuji, aware of this issue, convened a meeting with public security personnel, including Director Wu Bangzhou of the Vocational Training Center, the day before yesterday. They agreed on four measures: (1) All police officers, whether on duty or off duty, must immediately arrest any beggars they see, bring them to the station, and send them to the center for accommodation, without any excuses. (2) A patrol team will be dispatched once a week to search for beggars inside and outside the city. (3) Superiors will inspect each area to assess the presence of beggars as part of performance evaluation. (4) Crippled beggars unable to walk will be transported to the center by vehicles hired by the bureau. All public security branch bureaus are now implementing these measures in accordance with the guidelines.

County Government Autopsy of a Strangulation Victim. A male corpse was discovered the day before yesterday in the Xiaochangbang within Miaojialong of Nanyan City, under the county's jurisdiction. The corpse was approximately thirty years old, with a blue cloth Tonghai satchel wrapped around its neck and hemp rope binding both hands behind its back. The local head of the village, Chen Shibaobao, reported the incident to the county and requested an autopsy. Yesterday morning at 8 AM, Judge Yu, accompanied by Coroner Shen, conducted the autopsy. The autopsy revealed that the deceased had been strangled to death. There were no other injuries on the body. Since no family members claimed the body, photographs were taken, and the body was placed in a coffin and buried after decomposition.

Changzhou 71

District Chief Liu Baorun Accused and Detained. Liu Baorun, the district chief of the Fourth District of Wuyi County, has recently been accused before the Provincial Government and the High Court. Upon receiving orders, the county government summoned the district chief to the county for transfer to the court for interrogation. On the 7th, at 1 PM, a messenger was instructed to summon District Chief Liu to the county for a conversation. After Liu met and briefly spoke with County Magistrate Wu, the police were instructed to take Liu into custody and immediately hand him over to the court for investigation. He was then detained.

Summary of Party and Government Talks. The Wuyi County Party and Government Talks were held at the county government at 2 PM on the 7th to discuss various issues. (1) The Committee for Overdue Grain Transport Debts decided to urge the Finance Bureau to expedite the matter and requested the bureau to convene a meeting with the county government, the county party headquarters, and the various bureaus of the county to discuss and draft simple regulations for organizational establishment. (2) It was decided that the Education Bureau should negotiate with the Chamber of Commerce to take over the library managed by the Chamber of Commerce. (3) Regarding the Boy Scout funding, it was decided that the Finance Bureau should allocate funds immediately.

Continuing the Police Training Class. The first session of the Police Training Class of the Wuyi County Public Security Bureau has already graduated. After Director Liu took office, he continued to operate the program. He has now instructed the various branch bureaus and substations to select trainees for the second session, who are scheduled to report on the 15th of this month. Xu Chuzhi will continue to be appointed as the director of education, in charge of all matters.

Jiangyin 72

The Red Pill Case is Handled by the Judiciary. Magistrate Li previously received an order from the Provincial Government, in the name of the Provincial Committee, accompanied by the Provincial Police Team, to go to Zhangqing Township, Zhashang, to investigate and confiscate the Red Pill apparatus. Zhao Zifang, the deputy commander of the defense corps, Jiang Yizun, the assistant officer of the Seventh District Office, and team member Jiang Weisheng were suspected of committing offenses and were temporarily placed under the custody of the Provincial Police Team at the Confucian Temple. Now that Magistrate Li has taken over the affairs, he has received instructions from the Department of Civil Affairs that the case is to be handled by the judiciary. The Provincial Police Team has departed for Nantong to maintain order. On the evening of the 6th, Jiang Yizun and the other two individuals were escorted to the county government. The Provincial Police Team departed for Nantong on the morning of the 7th. Further news: The Department of Civil Affairs has ordered that the Red Pill case in Zhangqing Township be handled by the judiciary. At around 3 PM on the 7th, Magistrate Li and Judge Yang secretly interrogated the suspects in the reception room, barring onlookers. They interrogated Jiang Yizun, Zhao Zhifang, and Jiang Weisen. It is said that the three did not admit to knowing about the Red Pill affair and provided no concrete confessions. The interrogator challenged them, asking why they (referring to Jiang Yizun) led the search, which resulted in the discovery of empty boxes of white powder, and several families were found to have the same empty boxes. Jiang vehemently denied any knowledge. Next, they inquired about the number of firearms and personnel in the Zhangqing Defense Corps, as well as the number of firearms confiscated at Zhashang. After the interrogation, Jiang Yizun and the other two were allowed to be released on bail with guarantees from two shops and were required to be available for questioning at any time. In the meantime, Huang Bingzhong and his son Huang Hehao were to be summoned for interrogation. As Jiang and the others had no shopkeepers to provide guarantees, they were ordered to be detained.

The County Party Headquarters Resolves the Issue of Holiday Wages. The County Party Headquarters Steering Committee convened a meeting of managers from various cloth factories on the 6th to discuss the issue of paying holiday wages. They discussed paying regular wages for holidays, paying double wages for May Day, and paying attention to worker hygiene, as well as discussing implementation methods. Those who work as usual on May Day, in addition to the regular holiday wages, will still be paid wages for the cloth they weave according to the usual factory rules. All overdue wages for the New Year's Day, March 12th, and March 29th holidays should be paid in full by May 9th. Factories that lay off workers should comply with the Worker Protection Law promulgated by the Central Government.

Reactionary Slogans Appear in Qingyang Township. Qingyang Township is a major town in Jiangyin, with a dense population and located in the center of Chengxi. Recently, many reactionary slogans have appeared there. Residents of the area are flocking to Chengxi and the two counties to avoid danger. The Second Public Security Branch Bureau and the Defense Corps have taken strict precautions.

Jingjiang 73

Bandits Continue to Riot in the Eastern Countryside. On the afternoon of the 6th, over a thousand bandits from Taixing crossed the river by ferry from Wangjiashi. They first went to the Wenwu Temple to burn it down. The guerrilla force stationed in Changan City went to assist upon hearing the news but retreated due to being outnumbered. The bandits entered Changan City, and the government troops retreated to Xiaoshi. Ye Xiuyi's residence was completely destroyed by the bandits. Upon receiving the report, the county government immediately dispatched a team to assist overnight. The bandits have since returned to the north of the river.

Zhang Zhongxi Kidnapped by Bandits. Zhang Zhongxi, a native of Houhe City, owns most of his ancestral farmland in the Baimuqiao area west of Lishi Bridge. Therefore, Zhang often resides in the western countryside. Unexpectedly, in the middle of the night on the 4th, over ten bandits broke in and kidnapped Zhang. He was taken to Dagang by public ferry to an unknown destination.

Traces of Bandits Still in Jiashi City. Because the Defense Corps and the Public Security Branch Bureau successively defected in Jiashi City, over forty stores were looted, and the market remains desolate. At 1 AM on the morning of the 5th, gunshots were heard again. The government troops came out to suppress the bandits upon hearing the gunshots, and the bandits retreated. The Huangyu Rice Store on North Street was looted, and the store owner Huang Qishan was kidnapped. He has not yet escaped danger.

Nanhui 74

New Disputes Over the Pujigong Land. The Pujigong land has been coveted and subsequently vandalized, resulting in lawsuits for decades. The cases have piled up like mountains. Recently, large-scale activities have resumed, causing Ji Qingren, the chairman of the Basic Management Committee in charge of the property, to focus all his efforts on dealing with the situation to protect the property rights. The notice is recorded below. It has been found that the association controls 307 mu, 6 fen, and 0.08 mao of Pujiwang and Li Liangtang foot land, and on July 17th of the Republic of China 15th year, it went through legal procedures and obtained a Ministry license from the former Jiangsu Shatians Administration. However, recently, unscrupulous people have incited tenants, hoping to steal and buy, and take profits from it, which is absurd. A special notice is issued to all Pujigong tenants, who must know that the association holds the Ministry license for this property, which is a formal public property. How can it be allowed to be stolen and sold? All tenants must not be fooled, so as not to regret it.

Zhenjiang 75

All Rice Transport in Jiangsu Province is Tax-Exempt. The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce, considering the poor harvest last year and the people's food shortage, telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, requesting that all customs offices in Jiangsu Province and special financial commissioners be ordered to exempt taxes on the purchase of rice and stones with passports issued by the provincial government to aid people's food. A reply was received from the Ministry of Finance approving the request, but it stipulated that transporting rice to disaster areas to aid disaster victims must be reported to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for record-keeping.

Distributing the Second Batch of Compensation for the Benniu Disaster. The second batch of compensation for the Benniu Wheel Disaster was originally scheduled to be distributed at the end of March this year. At the beginning of last month, the families of the victims came to Zhenjiang to collect the compensation. However, the responsible party, Yu Shicheng, repeatedly delayed the process. Yesterday, the families of the victims, due to the busy farming season, gathered at Yu's residence to demand payment. Yu, seeing the tense situation and unable to make excuses, raised the cash and led the families to the Chamber of Commerce for distribution. This time, the compensation was based on the certificates issued last year, stating that each household would receive 168 yuan, 2 jiao, and 4 fen, which had been reported to the Department of Civil Affairs and the Department of Construction for record-keeping. Unexpectedly, Yu suddenly denied the previous agreement and shortchanged each household by 21 yuan, 1 jiao, and 8 fen, totaling 1,800 yuan for 85 households. The families of the victims protested in vain and originally planned to go to the Department of Civil Affairs and the Department of Construction to petition, but due to the busy farming season, they had to return home to cultivate the land and had no choice but to accept the injustice. It is reported that the Department of Civil Affairs, the Department of Construction, and the County Party Headquarters believed that the case had already been decided, how could Yu be allowed to overturn it on his own, and have strictly ordered Yu to make up the full amount.

Yangzhou 76

The End of Conscripted Labor for Road Construction. The county received instructions from the Provincial Construction Department, stating that as the busy farming season has arrived, the conscripted labor for road construction should be temporarily concluded, and the Conscripted Labor for Road Construction Coordination Association and the office, or the conscripted labor assistant, should be abolished. Yesterday (the 6th), it was specially instructed to the Construction Bureau to comply and complete the Yanghuo Road project within a limited time to complete it and report it to the Department.

Construction of the Xiong Garden Has Begun. The Xiong Martyr's Cemetery Committee held its first regular meeting yesterday (the 5th) afternoon. A total of more than 30 committee members attended and were present. Chairman Wang Boling resolved a total of 19 cases. It was decided that construction should begin immediately with the more than 28,000 yuan already raised and that it should be completed within one year. Plans will be solicited and bidding will be invited within the day.

The Opposition to the Electricity Price Increase Has Ended. The local Zhenyang Electric Light Company has caused a unified opposition from the Pi Industry and 35 other industries due to the illegal price increase and suspension of fuel payments. It is now heard that the Chamber of Commerce and the Association of Commerce Association convened representatives of both parties at the Chamber of Commerce yesterday (the 6th) afternoon to discuss a solution. As a result, it was agreed that the price for those who burn fire meters should be 2 jiao and 2 fen per degree, and the price for sitting lamps should be 1 yuan, 3 jiao, and 2 fen per lamp per month. The excess payment collected by the company due to the illegal price increase without consent will be allocated to offset the streetlight fuel payment. At that time, a contract was signed and complied with. In addition, it is also heard that the company plans to use 2,000 yuan to compensate the other party for the losses incurred.

Funing 77

Rescue of a Kidnapping Victim. On the night of April 28th, Tang Li'an, a patrolman from the Fourth Police Station of the Seventh District, encountered more than ten bandits carrying a young child while patrolling near the Longwang Nunnery. He fired his gun to attack. Unable to withstand the force, the bandits fled eastward. Patrolman Tang led the police to chase for six or seven li. There happened to be a small river, and the bandits abandoned the child and fled across the water. When the police chased after them, they had no boat to cross the river and had to take the child back. The child's name was Lu Nianfu, five years old, from Yuandaogang, Yancheng. He has now been taken back to be cared for by his father, Lu Yantong.

The Police Force Kills Prominent Bandits. In Yangjia She, in the western countryside of Funing, there are small groups of bandits lurking. Xiong Yanghe, the director of the Public Security Bureau and the captain of the police brigade, secretly sent police squad leader Li Yuzhi and others to encircle and suppress them. At dawn on April 29th, they opened fire with the bandits, killing one bandit on the spot and seizing a box gun. Two bandits, Zhou Guiyin and Xu Futang, were captured alive. The remaining bandits fled in all directions. A 20-year-old woman named Qiu was found in the bandit's den. Sun Qilian, the patrolman of the police team, was also shot in the shoulder during the battle. It is reported that the bandit who was killed, Yang Shaoxian, was a prominent bandit. The police team has now escorted the captured bandits Zhou Guiyin and the abducted woman Qiu to the county government for interrogation.

Robbery Cases Occur Frequently in the Four Rural Districts. The home of Yao Zengshou, a farmer residing in Nanrunwei, Yongqi District, was suddenly robbed at around 11 PM on the 4th. The victim was beaten by the robbers. It is learned that after the county's examination, the victim's injuries were minor. Furthermore, Gao Yuefan, a farmer residing in Yuxue Village, Tianwang District, was suddenly visited by more than ten robbers wielding knives and clubs at around 3 PM on the 4th. They beat the victim Gao Jingren and stole six gold rings, more than 200 yuan in silver dollars, and clothing worth approximately 1,000 yuan in total. In addition, the home of Lu Baosheng in Xizangwei was suddenly visited by more than ten robbers at around 10 PM on the 5th. They stole more than ten shi of rice and clothing worth several hundred yuan. All the victims have requested that the robbers be arrested.

Order to Investigate the Misdeeds of the Head of the Chamber of Commerce in Xitang. Pinghu 79

Recent News on the Twin Pagodas Problem. The twin pagodas in front of the North Temple in this county were built in the Tang Dynasty and are indeed historical sites. However, due to years of disrepair, they are on the verge of collapse and are quite dangerous. Recently, the residents of the county have been divided into two factions regarding the problem of demolishing the pagodas: one advocates for preservation, and the other advocates for demolition. The dispute is endless. Shanghai notables, such as Wang Yiting, have telegraphed the Ministry of the Interior, requesting that the county preserve them in accordance with the regulations on the preservation of antiquities and historical sites. Zhu Jiahua, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs, believes that the ancient pagodas should be preserved, and he has ordered Fang Li to report the facts truthfully for review.

Appointment of the Inland River Police Captain in Pinghu. Hu Zhengbin, the captain of the Ninth Inland River Police Team stationed in Pinghu, was previously transferred to serve as the captain of the Third Team of the First District by order of the province. The vacancy was filled by Shi Guotai. Captain Shi took over the affairs yesterday (the 6th).

Xiaoshan 80

Meeting to Allocate Construction Bonds. The Xiaoshan County Government has been assigned 160,000 yuan in construction bonds by the province. County Magistrate Du convened a meeting with party, government, and various groups of gentry at the County Chamber of Commerce the other day to discuss and decide on the allocation. The southeast and eastern regions will each recognize one-third, and the urban area and northwest region will recognize one-third. The method is that each household with more than 20 mu of farmland will recognize 3 jiao, those with more than 50 mu of sandy land will recognize 1 jiao, and businesses will recognize 1 yuan for every 100 yuan.

Petition to Punish County Magistrate Du for Abuse of Power. The District Party Headquarters of the Second District of Xiaoshan believes that County Magistrate Du Shihua abused his power and illegally arrested Shen Zengfeng, a party member of the district, and detained him for as long as ten days, which is an illegal arrest. It should be petitioned to the higher-level party headquarters to severely punish the county magistrate in accordance with party discipline. This has been resolved by the general meeting of party members in the entire district: (1) Petition the County Executive Committee to forward a letter to the County Supervisory Committee to impose party disciplinary action. (2) Petition the County Executive Committee to forward it to the Provincial Executive Committee and then to the Provincial Government to impose administrative sanctions.

Shaoxing 81

Repairing the Pond Dike in Dezheng Township. The pond dikes in Dezhen Miao Wu Wanggong and other places were destroyed by floods and have not yet been repaired. The Construction Bureau has now sent personnel to carry money to carry out work relief and repair the pond dikes.

Hiring Staff to Raise Construction Bonds. Shaoxing has been assigned to raise 800,000 yuan of Zhejiang Province Construction Bonds. County Magistrate Tang has organized a promotion committee to handle it. The matter is divided into ten districts in the entire county. In addition to the urban area, Sun Deqing, Zhang Zijie, and other eighteen people have been appointed as fundraisers in each district. As the funds are large and the deadline is approaching, it is urgent to prepare quickly. Yesterday, the county government sent a letter of employment, and it will proceed in accordance with the regulations.

Petition for Gradual Ban on Tinfoil. Shaoxing tinfoil is a large product, and no less than 300,000 young men and women depend on this for their livelihood. Recently, due to the Ministry of the Interior issuing an order to ban the operation of superstitious items, with a one-year deadline for banning, without planning other ways to make a living, tens of thousands of workers have no alternative occupations, directly cutting off the livelihoods of the poor and indirectly affecting local public security. The County Chamber of Commerce is now appealing for the tinfoil workers. Yesterday, it specially prepared a document to petition the National Government for a gradual ban.

Hefei 82

Execution of Two Bandits by Firing Squad. The Fenglehe Town Chamber of Commerce in the southern countryside captured a notorious bandit named Wei Guangcai the other day, seizing three pistols and eleven bullets. He was handed over to the county. Yu Yincen, the head of the Northeast Four Towns District Corps, also captured a bandit named Cheng Jingwen, who had kidnapped Li Hengfeng's son, and handed him over to the county the other day. After interrogation, both confessed to repeated robberies and kidnappings and were sentenced to death. On the morning of the 2nd, the two bandits, Wei and Cheng, were taken out and tied to the execution ground at Cai Datang and executed by firing squad.

Madam Ju's Martyrdom of Chastity for Her Husband. Sun Shaoyan, who resided at Deshengmen and had served as a county magistrate in Gansu, died of pulmonary tuberculosis on the 30th of last month. His concubine, Madam Ju, whom he had taken in Gansu, was inconsolable. On the 2nd, after completing her husband's funeral, she secretly took a large amount of opium, behaving as usual. The family did not suspect anything. It was not until she was poisoned in the evening and realized it that a doctor was called to rescue her, but it was too late. She died after 7 PM.

Educational News

Important News

Private Elementary Schools 83

Flexible Methods for Hiring School Principals

The Ministry of Education, based on the Zhejiang Department of Education's request for flexibility in the procedures for hiring principals of private elementary schools, has specially ordered the educational departments of various provinces and the educational bureaus of various special municipalities.

According to the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education's report, "According to the Jiangshan County Government's telegram, 'According to Article 12 (2) of the Private School Regulations, the principal of a private school is to be selected and appointed by the board of directors and should be approved by the competent educational administrative authority. According to the regulations, since the principal of a private school is selected and appointed by the board of directors, the approval of the competent authority is required. Whether the principal selected by the board of directors should be submitted to the competent authority for approval before being hired. Please request instructions. 1. After further investigation, Article 2 of the Private School Regulations stipulates that the Department of Education or the Education Bureau of a special municipality is the competent authority for private secondary and elementary schools. For private elementary schools in the county, the establishment and registration of its board of directors and school should be submitted to the Department for approval, and the principal selected by the board of directors should also be submitted to the competent authority for approval. However, in the event that the principal is incompetent, and it is appropriate to appoint a principal when the board of directors is suspended, whether the county government should submit a report to the Department for record-keeping, and at the same time order the board of directors to resume as soon as possible, and whether a qualified person should be selected for the position of principal and submitted to the Department for appointment, or whether the Department should directly select the appointment. Please request instructions. 2." Based on this, the Department believes that the approval and selection of the principals of private secondary and elementary schools must be handled by the Department of Education. However, there are quite a number of private elementary schools in the various jurisdictions, and the process of submitting requests back and forth is also time-consuming. What should be done? The details are hereby submitted for review and instructions." The principal selected by the board of directors of a private school should be submitted to the competent educational administrative authority for approval before being hired. However, there are quite a number of private elementary schools in various jurisdictions, and the approval or selection of the principals may be handled by the local municipal and county educational administrative authorities and reported to the Provincial Department of Education for record-keeping in order to save procedures. In addition to the instructions and distribution, you are hereby ordered to comply and order your subordinates to comply as well. This order.

Compilation of Important Laws and Regulations Issued by the Ministry of Education 84

The Ministry of Education has issued a compilation of important current educational laws and regulations to notify the provincial and municipal educational administrative authorities. The order reads: Since the establishment of the National Government, the educational laws and regulations have become increasingly meticulous. For the convenience of reference, the Ministry has compiled all the educational laws and regulations that have been in effect since the establishment of the Ministry until the end of March of this year.

A Review of the Second National Education Conference (11) 85

(3) Measures for Reorganizing Private Universities and Vocational Schools (1) Incentive Measures (A) For private universities, colleges, and vocational schools that have already been registered and have excellent performance, the central or provincial/municipal governments may allocate funds for subsidies at their discretion, or the Ministry of Education may transfer funds from various Boxer Indemnity foundations for subsidies. (B) If a college or a department has made special contributions to education and academics, the Ministry of Education or the provincial/municipal education administrative organs may commend them or provide subsidies. (C) For those with experimental properties and excellent experimental results, the Ministry of Education may commend them or provide subsidies.

(2) Measures for Rectification (A) Private universities, colleges, and vocational schools that have not been registered should be ordered to apply for registration within a limited time. Those who do not comply will be ordered to suspend operations. Those who comply and apply will be granted registration, granted probationary status, ordered to suspend operations, ordered to close within a limited time, or immediately shut down after inspection. (B) The Ministry of Education should send personnel to inspect registered private universities, colleges, and vocational schools at any time. If the content does not meet the prescribed standards or if the financial deficit is too large, the Ministry of Education should consider the situation and order them to improve within a limited time or raise funds to make up the deficiency. Those who violate the regulations will be warned or shut down. Those who do not improve after guidance will be warned. If the situation is serious or if they still do not improve after a certain period of time after being warned, they will be shut down. (C) Newly established private universities, colleges, and vocational schools should be operated in accordance with the laws and regulations of universities and vocational schools, and should first apply for establishment in accordance with the regulations for private schools. Those who violate this will be immediately shut down.

(4) Measures for Universities and Vocational Schools to Promote Education. Universities and vocational schools should use the following methods to promote education to the extent possible: (A) Public lectures, (B) Night school classes, (C) Scientific inquiry offices, (D) Various practical technology special classes, (E) Various practical academic guidance centers, (F) Publishing departments, (G) Exhibitions, (H) Summer schools, etc.

(5) Measures to Improve the Level of University and Vocational School Students and Seek Employment Opportunities for Graduates.

(1) Measures to improve before enrollment: (A) Raise the level of secondary schools, (B) Strict entrance examinations

(2) Measures to improve after enrollment: (A) Formulate curriculum standards, minimum graduation standards, and regulations for the qualifications of professors. (B) Teaching should focus on extracurricular self-study, experimentation, practice, and on-site inspection. Each course should refer to more than two reference books. University students should be able to write in the first foreign language and read in the second foreign language. (C) Emphasize daily grades, and conduct strict monthly and final exams. Students with excellent grades, or those with outstanding achievements in special research, will be given scholarships or special certificates. Graduates have priority in assuming equivalent public office.

(3) The Ministry of Education should investigate and compile statistics on the number of existing, currently needed, and projected future specialized personnel in order to establish standards for training specialized personnel. Expand enrollment where there is a shortage, and stop enrollment where there is a surplus.

(4) The government should order that those who manage technical and specialized undertakings must be university or vocational school graduates with considerable experience. All other agencies should give priority to employing university and vocational school graduates. The education departments of each province, the education bureaus of special municipalities, and other educational academic institutions or organizations should set up career counseling offices and give priority to introducing university graduates to serve. The Ministry of Personnel of the Examination Yuan should give priority to screening and sending university and vocational school graduates who are still unemployed to various places for employment.

(5) The Ministry of Education should, in conjunction with various specialized ministries, formulate the number of probationary positions and salaries during the probationary period for various specialized talents to be accommodated each year by national agencies, associations, factories, etc. Graduates of national universities and vocational schools who are willing to work should be registered in the Education Gazette by the Ministry of Education, consulted by various specialized ministries, and distributed to various provinces, agencies, associations, and factories to try out their skills.

(6) Increase the number of students sent abroad for study

(1) The number of government-funded students, majors, etc. to be sent abroad will be determined by the Ministry of Education based on financial resources and needs.

(2) Selection criteria (A) Emphasis should be placed on natural sciences and applied sciences to meet the needs of domestic construction and to reserve faculty for colleges of science, agriculture, engineering, and medicine in vocational schools and universities. (B) Government-funded students should be dispatched in consideration of the special needs of domestic construction. Each time, those belonging to science, agriculture, engineering (including architecture), medicine, and education should account for at least 70% of the total number. Self-funded students may study any subject according to their own wishes, but those who study science, agriculture, engineering, medicine, and education should be given priority for government funding or subsidies. (C) Government-funded students should be limited to those who are employed by national, provincial, and registered private universities or vocational schools, educational, academic, industrial and commercial institutions for research, practice, and service for a certain number of years, have made considerable contributions to specialized academics, and are proficient in the language and writing of the country where they are studying, and have passed the examination or review. The specific subjects to be studied must be specified during selection, and the specific problems to be studied must be identified within the possible range.

(3) The minimum qualification for self-funded students should be graduation from senior high school. When applying for a study abroad certificate, they must pass the language and writing examination of the country where they are studying. Those who fail the examination will not be given a certificate. In order to facilitate self-funded students to prepare for language, national universities should, within the possible range, try to set up preparatory classes for various foreign languages.

(7) Measures to Establish Vocational Schools

(1) Vocational schools may be established by the national government or by the provincial governments, as decided by the Ministry of Education. National schools should be located in the center of industrial development, while provincial schools should be determined based on the needs and industrial situation of each province.

(2) In places where there are universities, there is no need to set up separate vocational schools if specialized courses can be set up within the university.

(3) When establishing a vocational school, attention should first be paid to equipment. Schools without sufficient practical equipment should not be opened.

(4) Vocational schools may admit graduates of vocational courses in high schools of the same nature. (5) The curriculum standards of vocational schools should be connected with high schools, especially with vocational courses in high schools.

(8) Measures to Improve Moral Education in Universities and Vocational Schools (Compiled and supplemented by the Ministry of Education)

(9) Measures to Promote Academic Research and Reward Technical Inventions.

(1) If a national university has a fixed research budget, sufficient equipment, and professors in the school have made special contributions to a certain academic field, a research institution may be established at its discretion. (A) When more than three research chairs are established, it is called a research institute. When more than two research institutes are established, it is called a research academy. (B) The academy should be named after the school, the institute should be named after the college or department, and the research chair should be named after the course. (C) The president of the academy may be concurrently held by the president of the university, the director of the institute may be concurrently held by the dean of the college or the head of the department, and the tutor of the research chair may be concurrently held by the professor. (D) The qualifications of research students are limited to graduates of national, provincial, and registered private universities who have passed the examination. The research period is tentatively set at least three years. After the research period expires, they may take the national doctoral degree examination. (E) In addition to those who serve as teaching assistants or assistants in the school and concurrently serve as research students, a subsidy may be given each month at the discretion of the school. (F) If the aforementioned research institutions require a large amount of funds that cannot be saved, the redundant expenses should be reduced first and transferred for use. If it is not enough, a budget should be listed and submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval by the Ministry of Finance.

(2) The Ministry of Education should formulate regulations based on the central government's decision: (A) Regulations on academic research practice scholarships and subsidies, (B) Regulations on special rewards and protection for technical inventions and discoveries, (C) Regulations on subsidizing scholars' academic monographs for printing expenses. In order to encourage academic research, the Ministry of Education should also formulate regulations on subsidizing academic organizations. The above regulations should all raise funds.

(8) Plan to Improve Social Education

(1) General Outline

(1) Principles: (A) The administrative organization should be simple, (B) The implementing agency should be centralized, (C) The implementation procedure should be experimental first and then promoted, (D) Implementing talents should be specially trained, (E) Funds should be generously raised and their independence should be guaranteed, (F) The government should guide the society to promote it with all its strength, (G) Social education textbooks and various publications should be annotated with phonetic symbols as much as possible.

(2) Administrative organization: In addition to the social education departments or sections already established in the Ministry of Education and the provincial education departments, (A) the county education bureaus should set up social education offices or sections, (B) the competent authorities at all levels may organize design or research committees, (3) Implementing agencies: (A) General - public education halls (and farmers' education halls), libraries, museums, art galleries, gymnasiums, sports fields, public supplementary schools for industry and commerce, etc., (B) Special - asylums for the disabled, reformatories, revolutionary museums, etc., with public education halls (and farmers' education halls) as the center of implementation and experimentation. All agencies should unite with the public education halls and should also be linked with schools or other organizations.

(4) Implementation process: First set up an experimental agency, wait until good implementation methods are obtained, and training talents have been successfully implemented at the same time, and then add them in stages. (5) Talent training: (A) Provide a large number of working talents for various social education implementation agencies, (B) Provide social education research, implementation, and cultivate talents with higher academic knowledge. The aforementioned talents should be cultivated separately in specialized departments added to universities at all levels, and in specialized teacher training institutions set up by departments and cities, or trained in experimental social education centers.

(6) Funding methods: (A) The central government has previously clearly stipulated that social education funds must account for 20% of the total education funds, and education administrative agencies at all levels throughout the country should earnestly comply, (B) In wealthy areas, the amount of funds should be increased from 20% to 30%, (C) To organize large-scale social education, the central, provincial, and county governments should donate special funds as start-up funds or funds (D) Each time the central or local government raises various public bonds, 10% to 20% of the proceeds should be allocated to social education funds.

(7) Other methods of handling social education should be consistent with the relevant agencies and promote them with all their strength. (To be continued)

The important education laws and decrees promulgated by the National Government and this department are compiled into a book, named "Compilation of Current Important Education Decrees and Orders". The education laws and decrees promulgated by the former University Council, which are still applicable, are also included in seven books, a thick volume. It has now been published. In addition to distributing it, it is jointly requested to search for and discover a copy of the compilation of current important education laws and decrees for your information. This order.

Meeting of the Education Research Section of the Municipal Education Bureau 87

The Education Research Section of the Municipal Education Bureau held a meeting a few days ago, presided over by Section Chief Tang, and decided on the following work plan: (1) Regarding testing matters: A. Determine the standards, B. Apply the results, decompose the interpretation, remediation, and guidance steps, and handle the results obtained from past tests to explain the reasons for its formation. If the student's performance does not meet the standard, the bureau will find ways to remedy it and submit it to the Supervisory Office for on-site guidance. The results of the research and guidance will be published in the bureau's publications to expand research. (2) Regarding experimental matters: The experimental education of children with low ability will be submitted to the department affairs meeting by Section Chief Tang in conjunction with Xiong Wenmin. (3) Regarding statistical matters: A. Conduct various statistics of schools at all levels this year, divided into three types: municipal, registered private, and unregistered private schools. (B) Organize test results into charts and investigate the academic performance of children who have been subjected to intelligence tests to find their correlation number. (C) Graduate volunteer statistics are also planned to be sorted out. (4) Regarding editorial matters: A. The Shanghai Education manuscript will be sent by Section Chief Tang and Xie Tang respectively to invite contributors. B. Revise the ten types of supplementary reading materials for children in the lower grades.

Local News

Today

Commemoration of the May Ninth National Humiliation 110

Preparatory Committee Convenes Commemorative Meeting

To Be Held at 9:00 AM at the Penglai Theater

All Sectors of Industry, Commerce, and Education Will Not Take a Holiday

On May 7th of the Republic of China year four, the Japanese imperialists, taking advantage of the domestic warlord Yuan Shikai's attempt to establish an empire and the tense international situation due to the European war, coerced the puppet government in Beijing with the Twenty-One Demands, a secret treaty aimed at destroying China. They forced the government to recognize the Demands within forty-eight hours. At the time, Yuan hoped to seek assistance from Japan and signed the recognition on May 9th. This unprecedented humiliation has not yet been avenged. Today (the 9th) marks the fifteenth anniversary of the May Ninth National Humiliation of the Twenty-One Demands. The Preparatory Committee of the May Revolution Commemoration Day for all sectors of the city has specifically decided to convene a commemorative meeting for all sectors at the Penglai Theater at 9:00 AM. All agencies, organizations, and party branches at all levels must send four representatives to participate. The Municipal Executive Committee also issued a declaration to the public and comrades (the original text is very long and omitted). The central government stipulates that the "May Ninth" holiday will not be observed according to the holiday regulations for revolutionary commemorative days. Therefore, all factories, shops, and schools in the city will operate or hold classes as usual today.

Various Organizations Telegraph Requests 111

To Stop Yan from Intercepting Taxes in Jin

The Silver and Money Exchange Association telegraphed the Banking Association of this city, stating that there were rumors of customs revenue being intercepted. Concerned about the credit of domestic debt, a joint meeting was convened yesterday, resolving to telegraph the Ministry of Finance to express their opinions and to send a telegram to the Banking Association of Pingjin to make representations to the authorities nearby. The original texts of the two telegrams are recorded below: (1) Telegram to the Ministry of Finance: To the esteemed Administrative Yuan, Ministry of Finance of the Nanjing National Government: It has come to our attention that recent Chinese and Western newspapers have reported that customs revenue in Tianjin has been intercepted. Although there are declarations that 5% of the old tax will be set aside to protect foreign debt credit, the customs system is thus being undermined. Once a bad precedent is set, it will follow the same path as the salt tax in the past. Foreigners will be wary of this, and restrictions and precautions will be unavoidable. This will greatly hinder the future of customs autonomy and the abolition of unequal treaties. This is a cause for concern from a diplomatic perspective. Since the founding of the Republic, the domestic debt market has been greatly opened, scattered among the people, amounting to hundreds of millions. The reason why this credit could be gained and this achievement could be made is that the fund is independent and has been outside of factional politics for many years. If this system is now undermined, nominally intercepting customs revenue, it is actually shaking the foundation and the credit of public bonds will plummet. This relates to the livelihoods of individuals on a small scale and the destruction of the social economy on a large scale. There will be no recovery, and the entire country will suffer. This is a cause for concern from the perspective of the people's economy. Our country's production is lagging behind, and the poverty of the people and the danger of the nation have reached their extremes. Military and political affairs aside, if we want to revitalize the country in the future, we must seek construction. If we want to plan construction, we must rely on domestic debt. If we now shake the foundation of domestic debt, which has a proven track record, for no reason, then the people, learning from the past examples of the first-year public bond and the ninety-six public bond, will not consider any domestic debt, and all efforts will be abandoned. Considering the painstaking efforts of various leaders and giants to save the times, they should not be willing to do this. This is a cause for concern from the perspective of national finance. All of these points are based on facts and are universally understood. They are not alarmist words. We hope that you will listen to our words and change your course. Our association manages the financial hub, and it is our duty not to remain silent. We earnestly hope that you will consider this and work together to remedy the situation, thereby maintaining the nation's vitality and stabilizing people's hearts. We would be endlessly grateful. Signed, Shanghai Banking Association and Money Exchange Association. (2) Telegram to the Banking Associations of Pingjin: To the esteemed Banking Associations of Beiping and Tianjin: The following is a telegram sent to the Ministry of Finance: (See above). We respectfully request that your association make earnest representations to the authorities nearby. The situation is urgent, and we hope that you will proceed in unison and provide instructions at any time. Signed, Shanghai Banking Association and Money Exchange Association.

The Fund Custody Committee telegraphed the Jianghai Customs Second Five Tax National Treasury Bond Fund Custody Committee, stating that there were rumors of customs revenue in Tianjin being intercepted. The committee held a meeting the other day and resolved to telegraph the Ministry of Finance and send a telegram to the Banking Associations of Pingjin to express their opinions. The original telegram is recorded below: "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance of the National Government: Reports state that the Tianjin Customs revenue, except for the 5% used to offset foreign debt, has been entirely retained by Tianjin. This revenue is designated to be used to guarantee the various domestic debt funds in the custody of our association, with the right of preferential allocation. The amount of these bonds is enormous and widely circulated. Bondholders are not only prevalent throughout the country but also include enthusiastic investors among overseas Chinese and foreign merchants. Therefore, the stability of the fund has a significant relationship with the national economy and international reputation. Since our association has taken custody, we have been diligent and conscientious, earnestly hoping that the entire country, regardless of regional boundaries, will work together to maintain the fund, protect the rights of creditors, and demonstrate national credibility. If the bad precedent of interception is set, it will inevitably cause panic in the national economy. How can the government gain the trust of China and abroad in the future? Furthermore, the fact that domestic debt funds cannot receive the same treatment and security as foreign debt is particularly painful for the Chinese people. Our association's duty is to not remain silent. We earnestly request that you provide strong support to maintain stability and alleviate people's concerns. We are filled with anticipation."

The Commercial Consolidation Association telegraphed the Ministry of Finance and the General Chambers of Commerce of Beiping and Tianjin to request a stop to the interception of customs revenue in Tianjin. (1) Telegram to the Ministry of Finance: "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance of Nanjing: There are rumors of the Tianjin Customs revenue being intercepted. The merchants were shocked to hear this. It should be noted that customs revenue is designated as a guarantee for domestic and foreign debt funds, and a committee has been established to independently manage it. If this interception becomes a reality, then the financial and social economy will be destroyed, and the credit of foreign debt will be shaken. From a diplomatic perspective, it will give international powers a pretext, affecting the future of customs autonomy and the abolition of treaties. The magnitude of the impact is unbearable. We specifically request that you quickly take measures to maintain the situation so that the interception does not become a reality, people's hearts can be stabilized, and the country's future can be relied upon. Urgent telegram, respectfully requesting your consideration." (2) Telegram to the General Chambers of Commerce of Beiping and Tianjin: "To the esteemed General Chambers of Commerce of Beiping and Tianjin: There are reports of the Tianjin Customs revenue being intercepted, which is deeply shocking. It should be noted that customs revenue is related to domestic and foreign debt funds. If a problem occurs, international credibility will be lost, and the domestic social economy will be harmed. Moreover, in the future, if the government issues foreign debt bonds, the people will take this as a warning and regard them with fear. Its impact on future construction will be profound and significant. We respectfully request that you make earnest representations to prevent interception. We are filled with anticipation. Urgent telegram, awaiting your reply. Signed, Geng Yin, Shanghai Special Municipality Merchants Association Consolidation Committee."

Indian Merchants Suspend Silk Shipments 113

Chinese Silk Merchants Suffer Another Blow

The Da Wanbao reported that Indian import and export merchants in this city received a telegram yesterday (the 7th) from the Sino-Japanese Silk Merchants Association in Mumbai, stating that the political situation in India is serious, business in Mumbai is completely stalled, and it is feared that the situation will not improve in a short time. They requested that all export firms in that port suspend shipments of all silk goods from May 22nd to August 1st. After receiving the telegram, the Indian merchants convened an emergency meeting of export merchants in the afternoon to discuss the matter. After discussion, it was agreed that although the losses would be great, there was no other option but to comply with the suspension of shipments. According to statistics from the Indian Chamber of Commerce in this city, the value of silk shipped to India each month since January of this year has exceeded one million taels. If this suspension of shipments continues for a long time, the Chinese silk industry will suffer another major blow.
